{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-08-15 13:14:59","updatedTime":"2021-08-15 13:14:59","title":"Sony Electronics Introduces the New Interchangeable Lens Vlog Camera ZV-E10 for Vloggers and Video Creators","link":"https://www.sonyalphalab.com/?p=113793","description":"<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"> \n <p>The ZV-E10 APS-C Camera Delivers High Quality Video and Audio Performance, Vlog-Optimized Functions and Versatile Connectivity – Perfect for Video Creators</p> \n</blockquote> \n<p>Exciting news from Sony and this new <strong><a href=\"https://bhpho.to/3zHTgvS\" data-type=\"URL\" data-id=\"https://bhpho.to/3zHTgvS\">ZV-E10</a></strong> might be the best vlogging camera option available yet for those looking for the best possible quality and versatility without the full frame weight.. Going for a totally reasonable <strong>$698 US</strong> for the camera body this beast is going to be in seriously high demand very soon I believe!! </p> \n<p>The ZV-E10 is and evolved version of the ZV-1 and A7C from what I can tell so far. The downside of the <a href=\"https://bhpho.to/2TCc5RQ\">ZV-1</a> is the smaller 1″ sensor and lack of a blurry background and the <a href=\"https://bhpho.to/3i4hrP8\">A7C</a> is full frame requiring often heavier than ideal lenses… With this unit you can easily put on any e-mount lens to achieve the desired look you are after and APS-C lenses are in general way lighter than full Frame lenses. The A6400 which I own was the best bang for the buck option previous to this new ZV-E10 in my opinion! </p> \n<p>Check out the press release below and I will update this article as more info comes out…. </p> \n<h2>NEW Sony ZV-E10 Overview with Miguel Quiles</h2> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\"> </div> \n  </div> \n </div> \n</div> \n<p><em><strong>Press Release</strong></em>:</p> \n<p><strong>SAN DIEGO, CA – July 27, 2021 –&nbsp;</strong>Sony Electronics Inc. today announced the first Alpha series interchangeable lens vlog camera, the new ZV-E10. Designed from the ground up for vlogging and vloggers, the new camera combines Sony’s advanced imaging technology with extensive usability and a custom-built feature set that is optimized for video creators.</p> \n<p>At its core, the ZV-E10 features a 24.2-megapixel (approx. effective) APS-C Exmor<img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/13.1.0/72x72/2122.png\" alt=\"™\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /> CMOS sensor and BIONZ X image processing engine to produce high-quality imagery with high-sensitivity, detailed texture depiction and beautiful natural bokeh. Additionally, the ZV-E10 includes the acclaimed vlogging-specific features favored in the popular ZV-1 digital camera including “Background Defocus”<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[i]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;that can smoothly switch between a blurred (bokeh) and sharp background, as well as the “Product Showcase Setting”<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn2\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[ii]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;mode that allows the camera to automatically shift focus from the subject’s face to an object being highlighted.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>“With the introduction of Sony’s first interchangeable lens vlog camera, the ZV-E10, we are excited to meet the growing needs of today’s creators,” said Yang Cheng, Vice President, Imaging Solutions, Sony Electronics Inc. “The new ZV-E10 pairs the versatility and excellent image quality of a large-sensor interchangeable lens camera with user-friendly features that are specifically designed for vlogging, making it an ideal tool for video creators looking to transition to a more advanced set up.”</p> \n<p>The ZV-E10 features a video-first design in a lightweight form factor (approx. 12 oz. / 343g<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[iii]</sup></u></a>) and includes the popular side-opening Vari-angle LCD Screen that allows creators to connect external mics on top of the camera. This simplifies setup while still allowing users to see the screen in selfie shooting mode and from high and low angles.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>In addition to the screen, the ZV-E10 includes several other easy-to-use functions that are specifically designed for vlogging, including a new mode button located on the top of the camera that allows creators to easily change between Still/Movie/Slow and Quick modes with just one touch.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The new camera also includes advanced video features such as 4K (QFHD: 3840 x 2160) video shooting and Slow Motion with high picture quality (FHD 120p)<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[iv]</sup></u></a>. Electronic image stabilization with Active Mode<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn5\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[v]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;is also available and delivers stable video recording even while walking and shooting hand-held. Further, the ZV-E10’s advanced AF (autofocus) technology provides fast, precise AF with excellent tracking performance, as well as high quality audio for clear sound recording.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>Sony Vlog Challenge Contest</strong></h3> \n<p>Together with this announcement, Sony will host their second Sony Vlog Challenge Contest that encourages entrants to create a vlog that highlights something that they are the most passionate and enthusiastic about. The entry period is July 27 – September 27, 2021 and is open to video creators in the U.S. (excl. terr.) and Canada (excl. Quebec). See contest official rules&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.sony.net/united/sonyvlogchallenge/northamerica/en\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u>here</u></a>*.</p> \n<h3><strong>Creative Versatility</strong></h3> \n<h4>An Interchangeable Lens Camera for Expanded Creative Expression</h4> \n<p>The ZV-E10 allows the user to expand their creative expression by utilizing the ideal lens for each individual scene they want to shoot. The wide variety of compatible lenses in Sony’s E-mount lens lineup lets the user choose the perfect lens based on their creative vision.&nbsp;</p> \n<h4>Advanced Autofocus</h4> \n<p>Sony’s industry-leading AF technology enables the user to leave focusing to the camera so that they can concentrate on composing their shot. The ZV-E10 includes Fast Hybrid AF and Real-time Eye AF for video<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn6\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[vi]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;with Real-time Tracking<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[vii]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;that allows the camera to keep track of the subject’s face and eyes for fast and precise autofocusing even while recording on-the-go and in challenging environments. The user can also customize the camera’s AF settings, such as AF Transition Speed and AF Subject Shift Sensitivity, to choose the rate at which the camera shifts from one point to another according to their creative preferences.</p> \n<p>Additionally, the ZV-E10’s Touch Focus function allows the user to intuitively set the focus position by simply touching the screen. With one tap, the user can instantly shift the focus position from one subject to another – almost anywhere in the frame. This is available in both still and video modes.&nbsp;</p> \n<h4>High Quality Audio</h4> \n<p>Sony’s leading technology, thanks to its internal Directional 3-Capsule Mic, enables the ZV-E10 to capture crystal clear sound recordings that accurately capture the speaker’s voice and the supplied wind screen to greatly reduce wind noise. For expanded audio options, the ZV-E10 includes a Digital audio interface via Multi Interface (MI) Shoe and a mic jack to connect an external mic. The inclusion of a headphone jack allows the user to connect headphones to accurately monitor sound recordings. Audio output timing can also be set for Live or Lip Sync.&nbsp;</p> \n<h4>Putting the Subject First</h4> \n<p>When shooting in different settings with dramatic changes in light, the user can rest assured that the ZV-E10 will automatically correct the exposure, using an original Face Priority AE (autoexposure) algorithm capable of rapid AE transitions, so that the subject’s face is not over or under exposed. This allows the camera to detect the subject’s face and adjusts the exposure to ensure that the face is depicted at optimal brightness, even when selfie-shooting in scenes with extreme changes in lighting, and even if the subject’s face turns away momentarily from the camera. In addition, the camera features the same advanced color science from the popular ZV-1 to optimize skin tones for any subject in both still and video modes.</p> \n<h4>Cutting-Edge Video Features</h4> \n<ul> \n <li>Internal 4K movie recording through full pixel readout without pixel binning<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn8\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[viii]</sup></u></a></li> \n <li>High bit rate XAVC S<img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/13.1.0/72x72/2122.png\" alt=\"™\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /> codec<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn9\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[ix]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;at 100Mbps when recording 4K</li> \n <li>Slow &amp; Quick Motion<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[x]</sup></u></a></li> \n <li>High-speed full HD recording at 120 fps<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn11\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xi]</sup></u></a></li> \n <li>Interval Shooting<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xii]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;for stunning time-lapse videos<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn13\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xiii]</sup></u></a></li> \n <li>Hybrid Log-Gamma (HDR)<sup>&nbsp;</sup><a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn14\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xiv]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;/ S-Gamut3.Cine / S-Log3, S-Gamut3 / S-Log3&nbsp;</li> \n</ul> \n<h4><strong>Designed for Video Creators</strong></h4> \n<p>Users can comfortably operate the new ZV-E10 thanks to its easy-to-hold body grip and large MOVIE button that is conveniently located on top of the camera. &nbsp;When paired with the optional Shooting Grip with Wireless Remote Commander (GP-VPT2BT, sold separately), one-handed shooting is simplified with easy to access zoom, record and a customizable button. A recording lamp (tally light) is also provided on the front face of the body for an at-a-glance indication of recording status. A red frame on the LCD screen also appears while recording to quickly and easily lets the user know if recording is active when behind the camera.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>A unique feature of the ZV-E10 is the zoom lever that can operate optical zoom with power zoom lenses and Clear Image zoom with both zoom and prime lenses. Using Clear Image zoom, the user can zoom without losing video resolution to maintain full 4K video. The user can also choose from eight zoom speed settings for added creative flexibility.</p> \n<p>The ZV-E10 features long battery performance with enough power to capture up to 125 minutes<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn15\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xv]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;or 440 images<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn16\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xvi]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;on a full charge so the user can record for long periods without worry. &nbsp;When shooting indoors, AC power supplies like the optional AC-PW20AM can supply power, so the user can continue to record without worrying about battery consumption. &nbsp;Power can also be supplied through a USB Type-C® connector, allowing external batteries to power the camera for extended battery life when shooting on the go. To conserve the camera’s battery, the ZV-E10’s Vari-angle LCD Screen allows the user to put the camera into Power save mode<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn17\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xvii]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;by closing it and instantly turn the camera on by opening the panel.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>Stay Connected</strong></h3> \n<h4>Livestreaming</h4> \n<p>The ZV-E10 can also be used as a high-quality webcam or live streaming camera by simply connecting it to a PC or smartphone<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn18\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xviii]</sup></u></a>&nbsp;for increased mobility while streaming with no additional software needed. The feature allows the user to take advantage of the ZV-E10’s outstanding image quality and crystal-clear audio as well Face Priority AE and Soft Skin Effect while livestreaming or on video calls. The ZV-E10 supports standards used for USB cameras like UVC (USB Video Class) / UAC (USB Audio Class). The ZV-E10 also allows users to connect to a power supply via USB cable while livestreaming for longer usage. For added convenience, the user can assign this function to a custom button to start streaming instantly.</p> \n<h4>Easy File Data and Transfers</h4> \n<p>Using Sony’s Imaging Edge Mobile app<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn19\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xix]</sup></u></a>, users can transfer selected images and video files to a mobile device via Wi-Fi. This also allows the user to transfer RAW image files. After the camera has been paired to the Imaging Edge Mobile app, the files’ location data can be acquired from the mobile device and recorded. Users can transfer files from an SD card in the camera to a smartphone (mobile device) via Bluetooth even if the camera is powered OFF<a href=\"https://A6C636E4-CD35-4387-98D5-2712B38181BA#_edn20\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u><sup>[xx]</sup></u></a>.</p> \n<h3><strong>Pricing and Availability</strong></h3> \n<p>The new ZV-E10 will be available in black and white in the end of August for approximately $700.00 USD and $900.00 CAD. It will be sold at a variety of Sony’s authorized dealers throughout North America.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>A new kit featuring the ZV-E10 camera and E PZ 16-50mm F3.5-5.6 OSS power zoom lens will also be available in the end of August and will be sold for approximately $800.00 USD and $1,000.00 CAD. It will be sold at a variety of Sony’s authorized dealers throughout North America.</p> \n<p>Exclusive stories and exciting new content shot with the new camera and Sony’s other imaging products can be found at&nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.alphauniverse.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><u>www.alphauniverse.com</u></a>, a site created to educate and inspire all fans and customers of Sony α – Alpha brand.</p> \n<p>New content will also be posted directly at the Sony Photo Gallery.
